Source Code

These source-code files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology". It is believed that the original listing was preserved by AGC developer Don Eyles, copied/reduced by AGC developer Hugh Blair-Smith, passed by AGC developer James Kernan to collector David Craig, scanned by Gary Neff, and then passed to the Dibner Institute where unfortunately the high-quality scans were reduced in legibility as part of the online-presentation process, and the original scans discarded. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. The images from the Dibner Institute website, and unfortunately not the discarded original high-quality scans, though with a few high-quality replacement scans provided directly by Gary Neff, are now available at the Virtual AGC project website. Report any conversion errors to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

016184,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
016185,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     PINBALL_GAME_BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016186,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
016187,000005:                                                                                                  #                It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
016188,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13 and Apollo 14.
016189,000007:                                                                                                  #                This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016190,000008:                                                                                                  #                that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016191,000009:                                                                                                  #                requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
016192,000010:                                                                                                  #                original YUL assembler.
016193,000011:                                                                                                  #  Reference:    pp. 397-480 of 1729.pdf.
016194,000012:                                                                                                  #  Contact:      Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016195,000013:                                                                                                  #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo
016196,000014:                                                                                                  #  Mod history:  05/11/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
016197,000015:                                                                                                  #                05/14/03 RSB.   First draft completed.
016198,000016:                                                                                                  #                06/06/03 RSB.   Fixed a bunch of typos in the comments.
016199,000017:                                                                                                  #                2010-10-25 JL   Fixed directive (COUNT# -> COUNT* on p446).
016200,000018:

Page 397 

016202,000020:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016203,000021:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -- 4           DATE -- 27 APRIL 1967           ASSEMBLY -- PINDANCE REV 18
016204,000022:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY -- FILENE
016205,000023:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION -- PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016206,000024: 
016207,000025:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
016208,000026: 
016209,000027:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016210,000028:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016211,000029:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016212,000030:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016213,000031: 
016214,000032:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016215,000033:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016216,000034:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016217,000035:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016218,000036:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016219,000037: 
016220,000038:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016221,000039:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016222,000040:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016223,000041:                                                                                                  #  `EXTENDED VERBS').
016224,000042: 
016225,000043:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION `ASSEMBLY AND 
016226,000044:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION'.
016227,000045: 
016228,000046:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES --
016229,000047: 
016230,000048:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016231,000049:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES AN INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016232,000050:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016233,000051:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016234,000052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT `CHARIN'), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016235,000053: 
016236,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016237,000055:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT, WHICH
016238,000056:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016239,000057:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT `CHARIN') AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016240,000058: 
016241,000059:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016242,000060:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT `NVSUB' WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016243,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016244,000062:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE `NVSUB' AND `NVSBWAIT' (SEE
016245,000063:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016246,000064: 
016247,000065:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
016248,000066: 
016249,000067:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016250,000068:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016251,000069:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS TO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 398 

016253,000071:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016254,000072:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016255,000073:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AD DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016256,000074:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016257,000075:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS `V37' IN THE
016258,000076:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016259,000077:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016260,000078:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS `PINBRNCH' IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016261,000079:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016262,000080:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND `CADRSTOR' IS NOT 40.
016263,000081: 
016264,000082:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016265,000083:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016266,000084:                                                                                                  #  `NVSUB' AND `NVSBWAIT' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016267,000085: 
016268,000086:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
016269,000087: 
016270,000088:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016271,000089:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016272,000090:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO `ENDOFJOB'.
016273,000091: 
016274,000092:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016275,000093:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016276,000094:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016277,000095:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016278,000096:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016279,000097:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016280,000098:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016281,000099: 
016282,000100:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016283,000101:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016284,000102: 
016285,000103:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
016286,000104: 
016287,000105:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE `DSPTAB'
016288,000106:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  `DSPOUT' (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016289,000107:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE `DSPTAB' INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016290,000108:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016291,000109: 
016292,000110:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION --
016293,000111: 
016294,000112:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016295,000113:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN `STARTSUB'.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016296,000114:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016297,000115:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016298,000116: 
016299,000117:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 399 

016301,000119:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016302,000120: 
016303,000121:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST --
016304,000122: 
016305,000123:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016306,000124:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
016307,000125: 
016308,000126:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016309,000127:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016310,000128:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016311,000129:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016312,000130: 
016313,000131:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
016314,000132:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATOR'S RESPONSE.
016315,000133: 
016316,000134:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016317,000135:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHT
016318,000136:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016319,000137:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016320,000138: 
016321,000139:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016322,000140:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016323,000141: 
016324,000142:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016325,000143:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
016326,000144: 
016327,000145:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016328,000146: 
016329,000147:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016330,000148:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016331,000149:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE `NVSUB' (SEE
016332,000150:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016333,000151: 
016334,000152:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016335,000153:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE `DSPABC' (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016336,000154: 
016337,000155:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION `PINBALL NOUN
016338,000156:                                                                                                  #        TABLES'.
016339,000157: 
016340,000158:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016341,000159:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016342,000160:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016343,000161:                                                                                                  #  (Note that this doc by Green and Filene is/was available online at
016344,000162:                                                                                                  #  http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1706.pdf --- RSB 6/2004.)
016345,000163: 
016346,000164:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016347,000165: 
016348,000166:                                                                                                  #        "IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016349,000167:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 400 

016351,000169:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR."
016352,000170:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016353,000171: 
016354,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016355,000173:                                                                                                  #  (Note that the following has been COPIED from ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc,
016356,000174:                                                                                                  #  and not necessarily thorougly checked --- RSB 6/2004.)
016357,000175: 
016358,000176:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016359,000177:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   # +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016360,000178:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   # VERB CODE
016361,000179:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
016362,000180:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
016363,000181:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
016364,000182:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
016365,000183:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016366,000184:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016367,000185:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016368,000186:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016369,000187:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016370,000188:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016371,000189:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = HITEMOUT+1
016372,000190:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   # MODE CODE
016373,000191:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016374,000192:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016375,000193:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016376,000194:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR FOR CLEAR
016377,000195:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016378,000196:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016379,000197:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016380,000198:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS1) = MONSAVE+1
016381,000199:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016382,000200:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +11D            # 0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER 11-13, C RELAYS.
016383,000201:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
016384,000202:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016385,000203:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1.
016386,000204:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016387,000205:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = NVQTEM+1
016388,000206:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016389,000207:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016390,000208:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016391,000209:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016392,000210:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE                   # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016393,000211: 
016394,000212:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION.
016395,000213: 
016396,000214:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

016398,000216:                                                                                                  # DSEXIT         =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR DSPIN

016402,000220:                                                                                                  # WDRET          =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR DSPWD

016406,000224:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          # TEMP FOR CHARIN
016407,000225:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
016408,000226:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
016409,000227:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            # TEMP FOR +,- ON
016410,000228:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
016411,000229:                                                                                                  # DISTEM         =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERB
016412,000230:                                                                                                  # DECTEM         =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
016413,000231:                                                                                                  # SGNOFF         =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR +,- ON
016414,000232:                                                                                                  # NVTEMP         =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR NVSUB
016415,000233:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         # STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
016416,000234:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016417,000235:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
016418,000236:                                                                                                  # CODE           =       VBUF +2         # FOR DSPIN
016419,000237:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         # STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
016420,000238:                                                                                                  # LOTEMIN        =       VBUF +2         # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016421,000239:                                                                                                  #                                        # MUST = HITEMIN+1
016422,000240:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         # FOR MIXNOUN DATA
016423,000241:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         # RETURN FOR +,- ON
016424,000242:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5
016425,000243:                                                                                                  # ENTRET         =       DOTINC          # EXIT FROM ENTER
016426,000244:                                                                                                  # WDONT          =       DOTRET          # CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
016427,000245:                                                                                                  # INREL          =       DOTRET          # INPUT BUFFER SELECTION

016459,000277:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016460,000278: 
016461,000279:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016462,000280:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016463,000281:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016464,000282:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016465,000283:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016466,000284: 
016467,000285:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016468,000286: 
016469,000287:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016470,000288: 
016471,000289:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   # COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016472,000290:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   # BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016473,000291:                                                                                                  #                                        # RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016474,000292: 
016475,000293:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016476,000294: 
016477,000295:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016478,000296: 
016479,000297:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016480,000298:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR DSPOUT
016481,000299:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016482,000300: 
016483,000301:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016484,000302:

Page 403 

016486,000304:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016487,000305:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
016488,000306:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
016489,000307:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
016490,000308:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
016491,000309:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
016492,000310:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
016493,000311:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
016494,000312:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
016495,000313:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
016496,000314:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
016497,000315:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
016498,000316:                                                                                                  #  (2003 RSB -- The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism.)
016499,000317: 
016500,000318:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016501,000319:                                                                                                  #  A'S   SELECTS A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016502,000320:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016503,000321:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016504,000322:                                                                                                  #  C'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016505,000323:                                                                                                  #  D'S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016506,000324: 
016507,000325:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016508,000326:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
016509,000327:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
016510,000328:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
016511,000329:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
016512,000330:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
016513,000331: 
016514,000332:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016515,000333: 
016516,000334:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016517,000335:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
016518,000336:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
016519,000337:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
016520,000338:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
016521,000339:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
016522,000340:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
016523,000341:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
016524,000342:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
016525,000343:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
016526,000344:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
016527,000345: 
016528,000346:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016529,000347: 
016530,000348:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016531,000349:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
016532,000350:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016533,000351:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016534,000352:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016535,000353:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 404 

016537,000355:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016538,000356:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016539,000357:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016540,000358:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016541,000359:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016542,000360:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016543,000361:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016544,000362:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
016545,000363: 
016546,000364:                                                                                                  #  THE 5-BIT OUTOUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016547,000365: 
016548,000366:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
016549,000367:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
016550,000368:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
016551,000369:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
016552,000370:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
016553,000371:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
016554,000372:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
016555,000373:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
016556,000374:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
016557,000375:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
016558,000376:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
016559,000377: 
016560,000378:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016561,000379: 
016562,000380:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       --      BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016563,000381:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         --      BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016564,000382:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    --      BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

016961,000779:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
016962,000780:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
016963,000781:                                                                                                  #  PASSES
016964,000782: 
016965,000783:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
016966,000784:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
016967,000785:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

Page 420 

017254,001072:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017255,001073: 
017256,001074:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017257,001075:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
017258,001076:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017259,001077:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017260,001078:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017261,001079: 
017262,001080:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017263,001081:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017264,001082: 
017265,001083:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017266,001084: 
017267,001085:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M'S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017268,001086:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017269,001087:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017270,001088: 
017271,001089:                                                                                                  #  MIXED-CASE,           M'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017272,001090:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017273,001091:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017274,001092:                                                                                                  #                        N'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017275,001093:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017276,001094:                                                                                                  #                        P'S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017277,001095: 
017278,001096:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY
017279,001097:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017280,001098:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017281,001099: 
017282,001100:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017283,001101:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017284,001102: 
017285,001103:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017286,001104: 
017287,001105:                                                                                                  #  Q'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017288,001106:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017289,001107:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017290,001108:                                                                                                  #  R'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017291,001109:                                                                                                  #  S'S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017292,001110: 
017293,001111:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017294,001112:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMONENTS IN NOUN.
017295,001113:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017296,001114: 
017297,001115:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017298,001116:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017299,001117: 
017300,001118:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017301,001119:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
017302,001120:

Page 421

017853,001671:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOS VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
017854,001672:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
017855,001673:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
017856,001674:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
017857,001675:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
017858,001676:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

Page 446 

018482,002300:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018483,002301:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018484,002302:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018485,002303:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018486,002304:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018487,002305: 
018488,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION.
018489,002307:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018490,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
018491,002309:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
018492,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018493,002311:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018494,002312:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KIMONON.
018495,002313: 
018496,002314:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018497,002315:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018498,002316:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018499,002317: 
018500,002318:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018501,002319:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018502,002320: 
018503,002321:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018504,002322:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018505,002323: 
018506,002324:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOESN'T TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW.
018507,002325:

018632,002450:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018633,002451:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
018634,002452:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018635,002453:                                                                                                  #  
018636,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018637,002455: 
018638,002456:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018639,002457:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018640,002458:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018641,002459: 
018642,002460:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018643,002461:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018644,002462:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018645,002463: 
018646,002464: 41,3400           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018647,002465: 41,3401           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018648,002466: 41,3402           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018649,002467: 41,3403           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018650,002468: 41,3404           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018651,002469: 41,3405           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018652,002470: 41,3406           03410                           TC       DSPOCTWO                              
018653,002471: 41,3407           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB
