019062,002880:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 459 

019064,002882: 
019065,002883:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019066,002884: 
019067,002885:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019068,002886: 
019069,002887:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019070,002888:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019071,002889:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019072,002890:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019073,002891: 
019074,002892:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019075,002893:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019076,002894:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019077,002895: 
019078,002896:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019079,002897:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019080,002898:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019081,002899:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019082,002900:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019083,002901:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019084,002902:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019085,002903:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
019086,002904:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019087,002905:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARET'S DISPLAY
019088,002906:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019089,002907: 
019090,002908: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019091,002909: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019092,002910: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OF UPACT LITE
019093,002911: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019094,002912: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019095,002913: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019096,002914: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019097,002915: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND,
019098,002916: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR
019099,002917: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019100,002918: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019101,002919: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019102,002920: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019103,002921: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019104,002922: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019105,002923: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019106,002924: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019107,002925: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019108,002926: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019109,002927: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019110,002928: 
019111,002929: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019112,002930:

Page 460 

019114,002932:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
019115,002933:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019116,002934:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019117,002935:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019118,002936:                                                                                                  #  V'S ARE THE 7-BIT VERB CODE.  N'S ARE THE 7-BIT NOUN CODE.
019119,002937: 
019120,002938:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019121,002939:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS ---
019122,002940:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R'S ONLY.
019123,002941: 
019124,002942:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019125,002943:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019126,002944: 
019127,002945:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019128,002946:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019129,002947:                                                                                                  #  IF V'S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019130,002948:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N'S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019131,002949:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019132,002950: 
019133,002951:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019134,002952:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019135,002953:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019136,002954:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019137,002955: 
019138,002956:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019139,002957:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.
019140,002958:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019141,002959:                                                                                                  #  PROCED WITOHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019142,002960:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019143,002961:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019144,002962:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019145,002963: 
019146,002964:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019147,002965:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AND EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR).
019148,002966: 
019149,002967:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019150,002968:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019151,002969: 
019152,002970:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019153,002971:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019154,002972: 
019155,002973:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR `PLEASE PERFORM' SITUATIONS
019156,002974:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019157,002975:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019158,002976:                                                                                                  #  `CHECKLIST' NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE `CHECKLIST'
019159,002977:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE `PLEASE PERFORM' VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019160,002978:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS `PASTES UP' THE `PLEASE PERFORM' VERB INTO THE VERB
019161,002979:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019162,002980: 
019163,002981:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 461 

019165,002983:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019166,002984:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASED INT THE VERB
019167,002985:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019168,002986:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019169,002987:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
019170,002988:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019171,002989:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED BO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019172,002990:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019173,002991:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019174,002992: 
019175,002993:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019176,002994:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019177,002995: 
019178,002996:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019179,002997: 
019180,002998:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019181,002999:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019182,003000:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP

019289,003107:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO .
019290,003108:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019291,003109:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019292,003110:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019293,003111:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019294,003112: 
019295,003113:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
019296,003114:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019297,003115:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB.
019298,003116:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN.  SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE.
019299,003117:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE.  SET BY VERB 32
019300,003118: 
019301,003119:                                                                                                  #  L TO ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED).
019302,003120:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019303,003121:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019304,003122:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019305,003123:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019306,003124:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019307,003125:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019308,003126:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019309,003127:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019310,003128:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DTA.
019311,003129: 
019312,003130:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 1206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 464 

019314,003132:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019315,003133:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019316,003134:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
019317,003135:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019318,003136:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
019319,003137: 
019320,003138:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019321,003139:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019322,003140:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019323,003141:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DON'T SET DSPLOC TO 1 SO CAN USE
019324,003142:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATE MONITOR.
019325,003143:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019326,003144:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR

019655,003473:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019656,003474: 
019657,003475:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019658,003476:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD CRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019659,003477:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019660,003478:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019661,003479: 
019662,003480:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY TEH KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019663,003481:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
019664,003482:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
019665,003483:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERITTED ASLEEP VIA
019666,003484:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019667,003485:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019668,003486:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019669,003487: 
019670,003488:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019671,003489:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019672,003490:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019673,003491:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019674,003492:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019675,003493: 
019676,003494:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019677,003495:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019678,003496:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019679,003497:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019680,003498:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019681,003499: 
019682,003500:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019683,003501:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019684,003502:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019685,003503: 
019686,003504:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019687,003505:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
019688,003506:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019689,003507:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019690,003508: 
019691,003509:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019692,003510:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MAKE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019693,003511:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019694,003512: 
019695,003513:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY FO THE DSPLIST
019696,003514:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
019697,003515:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 473 

019699,003517:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019700,003518: 
019701,003519:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019702,003520:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019703,003521:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019704,003522:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019705,003523:    4443           10633                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019706,003524:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019707,003525: 
019708,003526:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019709,003527:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019710,003528: 
019711,003529: 04,2633                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019712,003530: 04,2633                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019713,003531: 04,2633           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019714,003532: 04,2634           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019715,003533: 04,2635           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019716,003534: 04,2636           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019717,003535: 04,2637           30001                           CA       L                                     
019718,003536: 04,2640           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019719,003537: 04,2641           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019720,003538: 
019721,003539:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019722,003540:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019723,003541:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019724,003542:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019725,003543:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019726,003544: 
019727,003545:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019728,003546:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019729,003547:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019730,003548:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019731,003549:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019732,003550:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019733,003551:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019734,003552:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019735,003553:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019736,003554:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019737,003555:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019738,003556:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019739,003557:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019740,003558: 
019741,003559:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019742,003560:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019743,003561: 
019744,003562:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019745,003563:

019895,003713:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
019896,003714:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
019897,003715:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
019898,003716: 
019899,003717:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
019900,003718:                                                                                                  #  
019901,003719:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROS THE `TEST ALARM' OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
019902,003720:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS `CAUTION RESET' TO 1.
019903,003721:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
019904,003722: 
019905,003723: 40,3646                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2                         
019906,003724: 40,3646                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019907,003725: 40,3646           56115        ERROR              XCH      21/22REG                              #  RESTORE ORIGINAL C(DSPLOCK).  THUS ERROR
019908,003726: 40,3647           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK CHANGED.
019909,003727: 40,3650           00004                           INHINT                                         
019910,003728: 40,3651           34742                           CAF      BIT10                                 #  TURN ON `CAUTION RESET' OUTBIT
019911,003729: 40,3652           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019912,003730: 40,3653           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT                              #  BIT10 CHAN 11
019913,003731: 40,3654           33735                           CAF      GL+NOATT                              #  LEAVE GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT INTACT,
019914,003732: 40,3655           71035                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
019915,003733: 40,3656           64735                           AD       BIT15                                 #  PROG ALARM, AND TRACKER.
019916,003734: 40,3657           55035                           TS       DSPTAB     +11D

019919,003737: 40,3662           65026                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
